CREATE TABLE maintenance(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), type VARCHAR(50), date DATE)

CREATE TABLE tire(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), brand VARCHAR(50), size VARCHAR(10), type VARCHAR(50))</t><s>alter table engine rename column type to engine_type</s>

CREATE TABLE tire(id INT PRIMARY KEY, car_id INT REFERENCES car(id), brand VARCHAR(50), size VARCHAR(10), type VARCHAR(50))</t><s>ALTER TABLE tire ADD COLUMN price DECIMAL(10,2)</s>
